      function appendScript(url, async, defer) {
        let s = document.createElement("script");
        s.type = "text/javascript";
        s.src = url;
        if (async) {
          s.async = true;
        }
        if (defer) {
          s.defer = true;
        }
        s.onerror = () => onErrorHandler(s.src);
        s.nonce = "";
        s.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
        document.body.appendChild(s);
      }

      function appendScript(url, async, defer) {
        let s = document.createElement("script");
        s.type = "text/javascript";
        s.src = url;
        if (async) {
          s.async = true;
